---
about_this_resource_text: '<p>Prof. Szolovits gives an introduction to disease subtyping
  and discusses collecting genome data, precision medicine modality space (PMMS),
  genotypes and phenotypes, and the history of genetics and genome sequencing. He
  also discusses the Framingham study.</p><p>Speaker: Peter Szolovits</p><p><a href="./resolveuid/f4c352d3571d69663920eeb70162c7cf">Lecture
  20: Precision Medicine slides (PDF - 1.6MB)</a></p>'

  <span m="524190">was</span> <span m="524370">funny,</span> <span m="524730">too.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="1372150">things</span> <span m="1372450">stood</span> <span m="1373740">back</span>
  <span m="1374190">about</span> <span m="1375180">60</span> <span m="1375630">years</span>

  <span m="1383890">this</span> <span m="1384100">works.</span> <span m="1385180">And</span>

  <span m="1976700">you</span> <span m="1976800">get</span> <span m="1977010">a</span>

  <span m="1978100">it.</span></p><p><span m="1980960">Once</span> <span m="1981320">the</span>
  <span m="1981440">proteins</span> <span m="1982070">are</span> <span m="1982190">made,</span>
  <span m="1983120">they're</span> <span m="1983420">degraded</span> <span m="1984650">differentially.</span>
  <span m="1986010">So</span> <span m="1986660">there</span> <span m="1986870">are</span>
  <span m="1986930">different</span> <span m="1987350">mechanisms</span> <span m="1988130">in</span>
  <span m="1988250">the</span> <span m="1988340">cell</span> <span m="1989180">that</span>
  <span m="1989390">destroy</span> <span m="1989960">certain</span> <span m="1990350">kinds</span>

  <span m="1991790">faster</span> <span m="1992780">than</span> <span m="1993020">others.</span>
  <span m="1993660">And</span> <span m="1993710">so</span> <span m="1993950">the</span>
  <span m="1994310">production</span> <span m="1994850">rate</span> <span m="1995540">doesn't</span>
  <span m="1995870">tell</span> <span m="1996110">you</span> <span m="1996290">how</span>
  <span m="1996410">much</span> <span m="1996680">is</span> <span m="1996800">going</span>
  <span m="1996950">to</span> <span m="1997040">be</span> <span m="1997190">there</span>
  <span m="1997430">at</span> <span m="1997580">any</span> <span m="1997790">particular</span>
  <span m="1998360">time.</span></p><p><span m="1999830">And</span> <span m="2000010">then</span>

  <span m="2270180">papers</span> <span m="2271500">back</span> <span m="2271890">in</span>

  <span m="2583140">or</span> <span m="2583260">25,000.</span> <span m="2584760">It's</span>
  <span m="2584970">whatever</span> <span m="2585360">we</span> <span m="2585510">know</span>
  <span m="2585750">about.</span> <span m="2586770">And</span> <span m="2587550">that's</span>

  <span m="2806730">locus.</span> <span m="2807760">So</span> <span m="2807870">you</span>

  <span m="2811740">your</span> <span m="2811890">genes.</span></p><p><span m="2813120">Copy</span>
  <span m="2813510">number</span> <span m="2813840">variations,</span> <span m="2815140">there</span>

  <span m="2816330">DNA</span> <span m="2817710">that</span> <span m="2818130">have</span>

  <span m="2821010">And</span> <span m="2821220">the</span> <span m="2821310">number</span>

  <span m="2822570">variable.</span> <span m="2823810">So</span> <span m="2823860">one</span>

  <span m="2826410">one</span> <span m="2826620">associated</span> <span m="2827310">with</span>
  <span m="2827520">Huntington's</span> <span m="2828090">disease.</span> <span m="2829330">It</span>

  <span m="2834300">certain</span> <span m="2834720">section</span> <span m="2835200">of</span>
  <span m="2835320">DNA,</span> <span m="2836400">you're</span> <span m="2836610">perfectly</span>
  <span m="2837210">healthy.</span> <span m="2837790">But</span> <span m="2837900">if</span>

  <span m="2848070">known.</span> <span m="2848790">So</span> <span m="2849030">copy</span>
  <span m="2849390">number</span> <span m="2849690">variations</span> <span m="2850440">are</span>
  <span m="2850560">important,</span> <span m="2851580">gene</span> <span m="2851850">expression</span>
  <span m="2852420">levels,</span> <span m="2852900">which</span> <span m="2853140">I've</span>
  <span m="2854670">talked</span> <span m="2855000">about</span> <span m="2855720">a</span>
  <span m="2855780">minute</span> <span m="2856080">ago.</span> <span m="2858030">But</span>
  <span m="2858270">the</span> <span m="2858390">trick</span> <span m="2858750">here</span>
  <span m="2859200">in a</span> <span m="2859680">GWAS</span> <span m="2860580">is</span>
  <span m="2860790">to</span> <span m="2860910">look</span> <span m="2861150">at</span>
  <span m="2861270">a</span> <span m="2861330">very</span> <span m="2861750">wide</span>
  <span m="2862200">set</span> <span m="2862740">of</span> <span m="2862920">genes</span>
  <span m="2863490">rather</span> <span m="2863940">than</span> <span m="2864690">just</span>
  <span m="2865050">a</span> <span m="2865110">limited</span> <span m="2866240">set</span>
  <span m="2866550">of</span> <span m="2866670">samples</span> <span m="2867290">that</span>
  <span m="2868080">you</span> <span m="2868260">know</span> <span m="2868440">you're</span>
  <span m="2868680">interested</span> <span m="2869190">in.</span></p><p><span m="2870300">Now,</span>
  <span m="2870510">the</span> <span m="2870660">other</span> <span m="2870930">approach</span>
  <span m="2871590">is</span> <span m="2871770">the</span> <span m="2871920">opposite,</span>
  <span m="2872650">which</span> <span m="2872820">is</span> <span m="2873000">to</span>
  <span m="2873120">say,</span> <span m="2874440">let's</span> <span m="2874770">look</span>
  <span m="2875220">at</span> <span m="2875370">a</span> <span m="2875430">particular</span>
  <span m="2876060">gene</span> <span m="2876600">and</span> <span m="2876810">figure</span>
  <span m="2877200">out</span> <span m="2877410">what's</span> <span m="2877740">it</span>
  <span m="2877890">correlated</span> <span m="2878550">with.</span> <span m="2879600">And</span>
  <span m="2879750">so</span> <span m="2879960">that's</span> <span m="2880260">called</span>
  <span m="2880590">a</span> <span m="2880650">PheWAS,</span> <span m="2881520">a</span>
  <span m="2882000">Phenome-Wide</span> <span m="2882960">Association</span> <span
  m="2883770">Study.</span> <span m="2885000">And</span> <span m="2885180">now</span>
  <span m="2885420">what</span> <span m="2885660">you</span> <span m="2885810">do</span>
  <span m="2886230">is</span> <span m="2886530">you</span> <span m="2886710">list</span>
  <span m="2887160">all</span> <span m="2887340">the</span> <span m="2887460">different</span>
  <span m="2887850">phenotypes.</span> <span m="2890340">And</span> <span m="2890520">you</span>
  <span m="2890640">say,</span> <span m="2890910">well,</span> <span m="2892080">we</span>
  <span m="2892290">can</span> <span m="2892470">do</span> <span m="2892650">the</span>
  <span m="2892770">same</span> <span m="2893100">kind</span> <span m="2893370">of</span>
  <span m="2893490">analysis</span> <span m="2894180">to</span> <span m="2894330">say</span>
  <span m="2895350">which</span> <span m="2895680">of</span> <span m="2895830">them</span>
  <span m="2896190">are</span> <span m="2896370">disproportionately</span> <span m="2897570">present</span>
  <span m="2898560">in</span> <span m="2898740">people</span> <span m="2899190">who</span>
  <span m="2899400">have</span> <span m="2899640">that</span> <span m="2899850">genetic</span>
  <span m="2900300">variant.</span></p><p><span m="2902490">So</span> <span m="2902910">here's</span>
  <span m="2903240">what</span> <span m="2903420">a</span> <span m="2903510">typical</span>
  <span m="2904110">GWAS</span> <span m="2904620">looks</span> <span m="2904890">like.</span>
  <span m="2905220">This</span> <span m="2905490">is</span> <span m="2905640">called</span>
  <span m="2905950">a</span> <span m="2906000">Manhattan</span> <span m="2906630">plot,</span>

  <span m="2908370">is</span> <span m="2908490">pretty</span> <span m="2908760">funny.</span>
  <span m="2909190">But</span> <span m="2909960">it</span> <span m="2910050">does</span>

  <span m="2933600">this</span> <span m="2933840">disease</span> <span m="2934530">and</span>

  <span m="2935520">have</span> <span m="2935730">this</span> <span m="2935940">disease?</span>

  <span m="2938370">this</span> <span m="2938670">gene,</span> <span m="2939090">whatever</span>
  <span m="2939570">it</span> <span m="2939690">is,</span> <span m="2940410">clearly</span>

  <span m="3114190">reduce</span> <span m="3114730">the</span> <span m="3115390">Bonferroni</span>

  <span m="3666270">W</span> <span m="3666690">and</span> <span m="3666870">H.</span>

  <span m="3947680">this</span> <span m="3947890">won't</span> <span m="3948130">be</span>
  <span m="3948280">on</span> <span m="3948400">the</span> <span m="3948460">final</span>
  <span m="3948790">exam.</span> <span m="3950770">But</span> <span m="3951130">look</span>
  <span m="3951370">at</span> <span m="3951460">these</span> <span m="3951700">numbers.</span>

  <span m="4246640">what</span> <span m="4246880">kind</span> <span m="4247210">of</span>
  <span m="4247300">data</span> <span m="4247690">it</span> <span m="4247810">is.</span></p><p><span

  <span m="4258580">is.</span> <span m="4259270">And</span> <span m="4259420">then</span>

  <span m="4261850">be</span> <span m="4262000">clever.</span> <span m="4263230">And</span>

  <span m="4556650">proclivity</span> <span m="4557310">for</span> <span m="4557520">something,</span>
